Local News

Li Jingcong Talks About His Experience with the Northwest Test Flight 156

(Continued from yesterday)

A Glimpse of Xinjiang Province: Although Xinjiang Province is located in a remote border area, its land is vast, its resources are abundant, and its reserves are rich, surpassing any other province in the interior. This is why outsiders covet it. As the saying goes, "Elephants are burned because of their tusks." If the Chinese people continue to ignore the situation in the province and do not seek ways to develop it, I fear that the near future will repeat the fate of the Northeast. If the Northwest, the screen of the country, is lost, then Gansu, Shaanxi, and even the interior provinces will be in danger one by one. I will not hesitate to be detailed and briefly describe the situation in the Northwest as far as I know. (1) Ethnic groups: According to the investigation, the total population of Xinjiang Province is no more than four million. Han people account for about one-fifth, all of whom are immigrants. The rest are Uyghurs, Hui, Mongols, and White Russians who fled in after the European War. All ethnic groups maintain their inherent etiquette, religion, and dialects. Although they are all happy and prosperous and do not infringe on each other, the Hui people do not have a very harmonious relationship with the Han people due to historical reasons, and they also account for the majority of the population. If there is no external aggression, this alone is enough to make Xinjiang Province unstable from time to time. (2) Culture: Although Xinjiang Province is the birthplace of mankind, it is impossible for new cultures from the outside world to enter due to traffic blockades. Also, because the land is vast and the resources are abundant, everyone has enough food and clothing. The old culture cannot be developed. At present, there are only a few primary and secondary schools in the province, and one Tianshan Daily. Higher institutions of learning are as rare as morning stars. When the company's plane arrived in Dihua on December 22, the Shanghai newspapers of December 12 and the Tianjin newspapers of December 19, as well as the China Weekly, were regarded as treasures and marked the beginning of a new culture in Xinjiang Province. As of January 7, when we left Dihua, the news published by Tianshan Daily was still reprinted from the news that we brought on December 20. (3) Transportation: Except for the dozens of cars owned by the provincial government, Xinjiang Province relies on mule carts and horse carts for ordinary long-distance transportation. Therefore, it takes seventeen or eight days to travel from the provincial capital to border counties such as Tacheng and Yili, and two or three months to reach Shufu and Heyu. Even from the interior to Xinjiang Province, it is not possible to travel in less than three months. Russia has built the Turkestan Railway along the border of Xinjiang Province and has set up many airfields. Therefore, Russia does not want to invade Xinjiang Province, but if it wants to invade, hundreds of thousands of people can cross the border in an instant. Even if we want to gather the military force of the province in one place in the shortest possible time and confront them, it is impossible. It is even more hopeless to transport reinforcements from the interior. (4) Production: The climate north of the Tianshan Mountains is cold, and the production of furs, feathers, and hides is extremely abundant. South of the Tianshan Mountains, the climate is warm, and grains and fruits are harvested every year. In addition, gold is mixed in the rivers, oil flows on the ground, and fuel is readily available everywhere. All kinds of metals are found throughout the mountains. In this naturally rich area, except for the Chinese people who are drunk with life and dreaming of death and arguing all day long, they do not know how to go there to develop it, enrich the country and benefit the people, and consolidate the border and defend the outside. Is there any reason not to inspire people's covetousness? (5) Commerce: What Xinjiang Province needs from the interior are silk, tea, ginseng, shark fins, cosmetics, daily necessities, etc. Merchants from the interior who transport goods go to the place of production and engage in exchange. Then, they transport the exchanged goods back to the interior for sale. The currency system in Xinjiang Province is different from that in the interior. Each tael is only equal to two jiao of silver, and the exchange rate is extremely expensive. It is not enough to make a profit unless they do so. However, this kind of exchange is ultimately inconvenient, so the number is very limited. In addition, soldiers and bandits appear and disappear unpredictably along the way, and it is easy to be robbed on the way back and forth, so merchants are increasingly afraid to make isolated bets. Xinjiang Province has no choice but to exchange large-scale cheap goods such as furs and cotton with Russia because it needs foreign goods. In order to realize its five-year plan, Russia does not want the goods of the interior to reach Xinjiang Province. Therefore, in addition to exchange, there are also regulations for cheap sales from time to time. For example, the kerosene sold in Xinjiang Province is better than that refined in the province, and the price is cheaper than that refined in Xinjiang Province. Another example is cigarettes, each box contains fifty cigarettes, which must be sold for four yuan in Russia, but only two jiao and five fen are sold on the Sino-Russian border, and the price is reduced to two jiao when transported to Dihua. If the Chinese people still ignore this and do not seek a way to save it, the commerce between the interior and Xinjiang Province will be completely destroyed.

Preparation for Launching the Regular Flight: Although this test flight was successful, there are still many things that need to be prepared for the official launch of the regular flight, and the difficulties are even greater than those of the test flight. In addition to reporting the experience gained from the test flight to the two general managers, we are now preparing a plan based on the experience in order to submit it to the board of directors for approval and start the plan. The outline is roughly as follows: (1) Ground equipment: The test flight results show that the line from Shanghai to Weitangzi, except for the Shanghai-Ping segment, is mostly high mountains and steep ridges, that is, barren wilderness. Especially the section from Langshan to the Tianshan Mountains, except for the weak water river, there are no human settlements, the climate is harsh, no grass or trees grow, and all living things are extinct. It is the most difficult and unsuitable air route for flight safety in the world. On this entire line, in addition to very proper radio equipment, climate measurement equipment, emergency equipment, health equipment, and equipment for parking aircraft and storing gasoline, there should also be traffic equipment, such as driving cars, etc., so that there is a possibility of rescue in case of emergency. Otherwise, it is not complete in terms of safety. However, from Guihua to the Sino-Russian border in Xinjiang Province, there are no trains or cars that can be used. The various ground equipment mentioned above can only be transported by the company's own cars, reluctantly. In the future, they will be left as traffic aids in remote areas. On the one hand, camels should be hired to slowly transport them. If there are no other difficult problems in the middle, it is estimated that it will take more than four months to complete the layout. (2) Selection of parts: According to the results of our investigation in Xinjiang Province, the number of valuable goods that can be transported by plane is very limited. Because there is not much commercial exchange with the interior, there are not many mails. It is decided to select the Junkers W33 No. 33 all-metal fuselage, which is not easily damaged and is suitable for long-distance flights, and the Junkers L5 No. 5 2-300 horsepower engine. With this aircraft, if the maximum distance can be set at one station every 600 kilometers, then in addition to the aircraft itself, the weight of everything is about 1,700 kg, plus about 600 kg for loading gasoline, the driver, and the radio operator, at least 6-700 kg of goods and mail or passengers can be carried. Compared with using a large aircraft, all expenses will have to be increased, but in reality, there are no such goods, mail, and passengers that need to be flown empty, which is not economical. (3) Funding: Whether this line can be officially launched five months after preparation according to our plan depends on the availability of funding. At this time, there is no certainty. The company is jointly organized by the Chinese Ministry of Communications and the German Lufthansa Airlines. According to the contract, the Ministry of Communications should recognize two-thirds of the share capital, and Lufthansa should recognize one-third. However, Lufthansa has been considering the opening because the Northwest route has no profit to be made and has no close relationship with itself. The Ministry of Communications is unable to pay at one time due to financial difficulties, except for relying on the government. This Northwest route, which is attracting worldwide attention, hoped for by the whole country, and related to the survival of the Northwest, although we have successfully test-flown it with the determination to sacrifice, may become a flash in the pan due to economic problems and cannot be launched. In addition, one more thing should be noted by charitable organizations: Since December of last year in Xinjiang Province, as of the day we flew back to the mainland, more than 3,000 young children have died of scarlet fever and diphtheria due to the lack of appropriate medicines for treatment. The new Xinjiang Provincial Government entrusted me to ask the Beijing Epidemic Prevention Office to purchase various medicines for treating and preventing these diseases when flying through Beiping and send them as soon as possible. However, the power of that office is limited and is like a drop in the bucket. It is feared that it will be of no avail. I hope that all charitable organizations will show mercy and quickly purchase medicines suitable for treating and preventing these diseases and send them directly to the "Xinjiang Provincial Government to be transferred to the Xinjiang Provincial Epidemic Prevention Bureau" for application. Is there any limit to the benefit of the elders and younger brothers in Xinjiang Province? Otherwise, it will be even more unimaginable when spring arrives. The best way to send it is to pack every two or three bottles into a small package, as a letter, marked "Via the Siberian route," and deliver it to the post office to be sent to the Xinjiang Provincial Government. It will definitely arrive within a month and a half. Otherwise, it will not arrive in Xinjiang for more than half a year. Also, small packages of letters should not be too heavy or too large, because Russia does not allow packages to be transported through the Siberian Railway to any place.

The Italy-China Express Ship Breaks the European Route Record 157

Can Reach Italy in Twenty-Four Days

The First Ship Arrives in Shanghai on February 2

This year, the Italian Post Company in this city has opened a special fast class for the China trade, stipulating that it can reach Italy in 24 days, creating a new era in the shipping industry between Central Europe. The following is a detailed report by the reporter after careful investigation. Company development: Since the Italian Post Company cooperated with the Italian C.osulich Line and then joined forces with the Italian Lloyd Sabando, its business strength has become stronger. It has concentrated all its efforts on operating the shipping industry between East India, Bombay, and China, so it has added new ships and launched special express classes.

Increase in Fast Ships: The company's postal ships in China originally had four ships, and the usual journey between China and Italy took 35 days. The company then changed and transferred two high-speed ships to China, one called the Conte Verde and one called the Conte Rosso. The Conte Verde had arrived in Shanghai earlier, and the Conte Rosso, which has a load capacity of 18,000 tons and can travel 20 nautical miles per hour, is scheduled to arrive in China on the first flight on February 10. After the new ship joins, the original postal ship Krakowiak will be withdrawn and will not operate.

Shorten the Sea Route: The first flight of the two express postal ships added this time will arrive in Shanghai on February 2, and the second flight will depart on February 8. The third flight is scheduled for March 11. From then on, the sea route between China and Italy can be shortened by one-third. The schedule of the fast class is now specified as follows: Shanghai to Hong Kong in 2 days, to Singapore in 5+ days, to Colombo in 9+ days, to Mumbai in 12+ days, to Port Said in 20 days, to Brindisi in 23 days, and to Trieste in Italy in 24 days.

Because Younger Brother Repeatedly Stole

Older Brother Conspired with Youngest Brother to Use Cruel Hand

Afterward, Younger Brother Returned Home to Tell Father

Older Brother Surrendered Himself to the Police Station

Wang Yunyu from Shandong Province resided in a shed at Number 6, Sanfuli, Sanyang Road, Zhabei, and made a living running a sesame cake shop. He had a total of five brothers. Among them, Wang Yungao, 34 years old, and Wang Yunbiao, 28 years old, were working as road construction laborers. Inspectors Wrongfully Detained by the Bureau

The Anti-Japanese Association believed that the store dared to violently assault inspectors amidst the serious outcry against goods, deliberately sabotaging the patriotic movement, and were truly public enemies of the people. In addition to confiscating all of the store's Japanese goods, they also detained the shop assistants involved in the assault, Liu Xiaochen, Bo Houzai, Yang Xiangyun, and others, and placed them in the association's Zhabei Investigation Office to await punishment. Case of Embezzlement of Funds to Aid Ma (Zhanshan) 166

Transferred to the Prosecutor's Office for Investigation

Wu Mengyan, principal of Mingde School in Sande Lane, Zhabei, is being privately prosecuted in the criminal court of the local court by student representatives Xu Hongquan, Tang Shiliang, Xu Dingyi, and others for embezzlement of donations. The statement roughly states that after the Northeast Incident occurred, due to General Ma Zhanshan's courageous resistance, the Shanghai academic community decided to donate funds to provide assistance. This school collected a total of 52 teams of donations, a huge amount, but Wu announced that only 1,782.40 yuan were received. However, this school's seven teams have already exceeded this amount, let alone more than 50 teams. He privately split open bamboo tubes in the school and did not replace them after splitting open the 52 teams of bamboo tubes, revealing a major case of fraud. All the thank you cards were reprinted by him from the Minyi Printing House. Investigation showed that it was evidence of embezzlement. At that time, the party committees of the fourth and sixth districts and the Anti-Japanese Association went to the school to investigate and found that Wu Mengyan had embezzled 2,117.10 yuan. The actual amount was even higher. A report has been submitted to the Municipal Party Department and published in the public report. Therefore, they demanded punishment. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zhen opened the court. The defendant hired a lawyer to defend, saying that there was no embezzlement and that the plaintiffs were expelled students. However, the students claimed that the defendant was slandering them. The judge then instructed that the case was not sufficient for private prosecution and should be transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation before further review. Then, the court adjourned.

German Dean Robbed While Walking at Night 167

Gold Watch and Eyeglasses Stolen

Total Value Over 300 Yuan

Mr. Lou Najun, a German and dean of academic affairs at the School of Engineering of National Tongji University in Wusong, arrived in Song by train from Shanghai at approximately 8:00 PM on the evening of the day before yesterday (the 21st). After getting off the train, because it was late, there were no rickshaws available, so he had to walk back to school. When he reached the corner of Taixing Road and North Tongji Road, four thugs suddenly appeared. They were wearing gray military uniforms and had symbols. They were holding box cannons and other fierce weapons, warning him not to make a sound. They took a gold watch worth more than 200 yuan, a pair of eyeglasses worth more than 30 yuan, and a gold ring and five or six yuan in cash from his pockets. After the robbery, the group left. After the thieves left, Dean Shi rushed back to the school and used the telephone to report to the Public Security Bureau's Seventh District and the Security Corps. The corps and police officers were dispatched to the scene, but the bandits had already fled far away and could not be pursued. However, this was not the first time that school staff members had been robbed in that area. Since the night of the 13th, when Lu Xixian, director of the school's middle school department, was robbed of more than 90 yuan in cash, other people, such as Dr. Tang, had also encountered similar bandits and were robbed of less than 10 yuan, so they did not report to the authorities. This was the third time that Dean Shi had been robbed. Tang Chengzong, commander of the Wusong Security Corps, in view of the endless robbery cases on Tongji Road, convened an emergency meeting of all the corps leaders and members at the corps headquarters last night to discuss defense measures to prevent future troubles.

Worker Commits Suicide Due to Poverty and Illness 168

New Ghost Under Xinqiao Bridge

Pity for Mother, Wife, and Children

At about 12:00 noon yesterday, a man resembling a worker suddenly jumped into the river under the Xinqiao Bridge in Yuncao Hamlet, Wusong. The men and women rowing sampans in the area saw it and rushed to rescue him. They rescued the man, but he was already at his last breath. Because the weather was cold and he had inhaled too much water, he soon died. A patrolman from the First Public Security Bureau of the Seventh District arrived at the scene. In the deceased's pocket, they found a pass issued by the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Administration, a half-body photograph of a worker's pass with the name Le Siliang written on it, and a piece of white paper with the address Number 1390, Xin Tao Yuan Li, opposite the Broadway Theater at the intersection of Huishan Road and Zhoushan Road written on it. The Public Security Bureau then contacted Zhao Maoqing, the head of the thirty-second precinct, and ordered him to go to Shanghai to notify his wife, Mrs. Yang, at the address. After receiving the news, she led her three children and Le's younger brother to Song. Upon seeing the corpse, they were extremely saddened and wept bitterly. According to reports, the reason for Le's suicide was that he was a laborer at the Zhanghuabang Railway Factory, and his wages were very low. He had an elderly mother above him and a wife and children below him, so his livelihood was very difficult. Recently, he had been ill for a long time. Yesterday, he heard the doctor say, "Your illness has been long-standing and will be difficult to cure in a short time. Moreover, the factory rules are now very strict. If you are sick for a long time, you will not receive any wages." Therefore, Le was extremely anxious. In addition, the end of the year was approaching, so he had the idea of committing suicide, resulting in this tragedy. The bridge was recently completed, and the completion ceremony has not yet taken place. It is also regrettable that Le Siliang jumped from this bridge.

Tan Zhiyuan Accused of Breach of Contract and Fraud 169

Tan Zhiyuan, an actor at the Star Film Company, was recently accused of fraud by Li Yuanlong, manager of the Dahua Company, and is under investigation in the Second Special District Court. Yesterday, he was summoned for questioning again. Plaintiff Li Yuanlong stated that on December 29 of last year, the merchant signed a contract with the defendant Tan Zhiyuan, inviting him to perform at the Nanjing City Grand World Theater for a term of two years. At that time, the defendant received an advance payment of 300 yuan and borrowed 600 yuan in advance, totaling 900 yuan, for which he issued a receipt. Unexpectedly, after taking the money, the defendant delayed going. Suddenly, on the 15th of this month, it was reported in the newspaper that he had another contract with the Star Company. The merchant was surprised and questioned him, but he avoided meeting. It was not until the 18th that he learned that the defendant was filming at the Star Company, so he reported to the police to arrest him and requested an investigation. The proxy lawyers Dong Chi and Zhang Bingyun supplemented the statement of the case, submitted receipts and other evidence, and requested incidental private prosecution to recover the funds. Under questioning, Tan Zhiyuan stated that he also had a contract with the Star Company for a term of three years, expiring on September 30 of next year. In December of last year, he went to Beiping with all the staff of the Star Company to film "The Teasing Marriage." After returning to Shanghai, he suddenly received stimulation and decided to change his career. This matter was learned by the Dahua Company, which invited him to join Dahua. He immediately stated that his contract with the Star Company had not expired and it would be difficult to agree. He also said that it would be possible to do spoken drama. As a result, they signed a contract with him, but at that time, Wu Chengyu, the perennial legal advisor of the Dahua Company, stated that the contract signed with the Star Company was for filming, and the current contract was for spoken drama, so there was no conflict. Therefore, he was actually deceived into signing it. Later, all the actors of the Star Company learned of this and cried and pleaded with him repeatedly, so he could not bear to separate and continued to work there. At this point, the official ordered the start of arguments, and the police lawyer Fei Xizhen argued that the law states that a contract is a contract. The police felt that the defendant had committed fraud, so they accepted the prosecution. To know whether the fraud took place, it must be proven whether it was intentional before signing the contract. Now, investigation showed that Article 5 of the contract signed by the defendant stated that during the contract period, he could not perform or film movies elsewhere. It was intentional beforehand, and then a breach of contract was implemented, obviously a fraudulent act. He requested that it be dealt with in accordance with Article 363 of the Criminal Law. At the end, under the defense of the two lawyers hired by the defendant, Zhan Jifeng and Yang Zhihao, Judge Zhang Shijie declared the debate over and scheduled a date for sentencing. The defendant was detained in the court's detention center.

Jianghai Customs Limits Registration of Customs Brokers 171

Deadline February 14

The Jianghai Customs Tax Department recently issued a notice stating, "For the purpose of notification, all Chinese and foreign commercial firms engaged in customs declaration business must register with the Customs before February 14 of this year. Those who have previously registered must re-register before this date. All application forms can be obtained from the Registration Section of the General Affairs Department of this Customs. The procedures are listed on the left. For domestic commercial firms, Chinese commercial firms should obtain a letter of guarantee, sealed and stamped by two reputable commercial firms, and submit it to the Taxation Division of the General Affairs Department of this Customs as a guarantee. This guarantee must also be signed and sealed by the Chinese Chamber of Commerce or the trade association to which the commercial firm belongs, guaranteeing that the commercial firm is a genuine commercial firm and does not engage in customs declaration business or declare goods for others. The validity period of this guarantee is limited to one year, and the guarantee must be renewed before the deadline, which is to be completed in January each year. The renewal procedure requires the guarantor to stamp the back of the guarantee, stating their willingness to continue the guarantee for one year. After the Customs receives the guarantee, the commercial firm must go to the Registration Office of the General Affairs Department to affix the firm's official letterhead and seal on a specially prepared card for record keeping. They must also submit two copies of the signature specimens of the firm's manager and other customs declaration staff. In addition, the firm must also fill out another form (Jianghai Customs No. 161) for the staff member authorized to sign and collect warehouse receipts, along with a photograph of the staff member, and submit them to the Customs together. The photograph must also bear the staff member's signature specimen. The procedure for domestic customs brokers is the same as for the aforementioned domestic commercial firms, but the guarantee item may not require other guarantees other than the guarantee that customs brokers should pay in accordance with the regulations.

Foreign commercial firms and customs brokers: Foreign commercial firms and customs brokers must submit a registration application to the Registration Office of the General Affairs Department. Commercial firms with consular representatives in Shanghai do not need this procedure. Commercial firms or customs brokers from countries without treaties should submit their application to the Shanghai Municipal Government Social Affairs Bureau for certification. The method of authorizing staff to stamp and collect warehouse receipts is the same as for domestic commercial firms.

General rules: All Chinese and foreign commercial firms that have complied with the above regulations will be deemed to have been registered and will be given a registration number. The commercial firm should then indicate the registration number in the upper left corner of the customs declaration form. All registered firms that subsequently change their name or nationality must prepare a registration application again, certified by the competent consul or the Shanghai Municipal Government Social Affairs Bureau, and submit it to the Customs for verification. (Omitted below) All merchants are expected to comply.

All Shuang Gong Silk Factories Closed 174

Result of Poor European Sales

In the past, there was only one Jinglun silk factory with more than 200 silk reeling machines. Eight out of ten of the Shuang Gong cocoons produced in our country were transported to France, Japan, and other countries. In recent years, due to the sharp increase in the sales price of Shuang Gong silk overseas, silk prices have risen daily. Chinese silk merchants have purchased machinery and added Shuang Gong silk factories. For a time, Fulun, Ruilun, Honglun, Xinlun, Jinlun, Hongshunlun, and others emerged. At its peak, there were seven Shuang Gong silk factories in Shanghai. Since last autumn, Shuang Gong silk has been affected by the cheap sales of Japanese silk, and European sales have gradually become sluggish. The shortage of Shuang Gong cocoons and high prices have caused silk merchants to suffer losses and unable to support themselves. Jinglun, Hongshunlun, Xinlun, Jinlun, and other four factories have successively closed between last autumn and winter. The three factories of Honglun, Ruilun, and Fulun have struggled to work, but because European sales have not improved and the accounting period is approaching, funds are extremely tight. Each factory has no ability to maintain operations and has successively suspended work since the day before yesterday. At this point, all seven Shuang Gong silk factories in Shanghai have closed down.

No New Personnel Will Be Added or Examined This Year

The Bank of Communications has always adopted strict standards for the recruitment of staff and employees. Examinations are held separately in Shanghai, Huha, and Han. More than 20 candidates who were selected were graduates of well-known domestic universities. It is said that the bank authorities have notified their subordinates to stop the examination and, from now on, not to add new staff and employees, in order to be pragmatic.

National Medicine Industry Opposes the Price Hike of Moutan Bark 179

The Shanghai National Medicine Industry Association, upon the suggestion of Executive Committee members Zhang Hongzhao and others, noted that Lexing (樂行) has been unilaterally raising the wholesale price of moutan bark (丹皮), engaging in unbridled monopolization. The closing price this year has soared to a staggering 150 taels of silver per dan, directly harming merchants and indirectly increasing the burden on patients. If this continues without intervention, it will negatively affect both commercial interests and society. With the year-end approaching, medicine shops will inevitably collect debts based on the unilaterally determined wholesale price of moutan bark. However, the National Medicine Industry Association is firmly opposed to the monopolistic behavior of the medicine shops. Therefore, the association, responding to the requests of its members, has scheduled an emergency meeting tomorrow afternoon to discuss effective measures to address the monopolistic price of moutan bark by the medicine shops. According to a responsible person from the association, if the medicine shops do not change their monopolistic stance, the association will take further effective measures to counter them.

Reader Communications

On National Goods Manufacturing 186

Qingguang

First, we must encourage all compatriots to not use foreign goods. The reason why our domestic products are not as good as foreign goods lies partly in the government's lack of emphasis on industrial development. However, the public's preference for foreign goods and their avoidance of domestic goods has an even greater impact. Even if domestic goods are not as good as foreign goods, if everyone uses them, manufacturers, in order to meet demand, will naturally strive to improve. Before the outbreak of the national crisis, only one domestic newspaper, produced by Tianzhang, was available. However, due to its poor quality, thick paper, and unclean color, the publishing industry did not use it. Consequently, Tianzhang's business soon failed miserably. After the boycott of Japanese goods last year, the publishing industry had no choice but to use it. As a result, Tianzhang's newspaper became popular again for a time. By the end of December, after only three months, Tianzhang's paper had improved greatly, becoming very thin and clean in color, indistinguishable from Western paper. This is because it received invisible support from customers. Therefore, in our opinion, to improve the manufacturing of domestic goods, we must first find a way to encourage all compatriots to not use foreign goods, thereby expanding the market for domestic goods. At that time, domestic manufacturers, in order to meet demand, will be able to greatly improve, catching up with foreign goods, like Tianzhang's newspaper. (C)

Letters 189

Dear Editor,

On the 18th of this month, your newspaper's local news column published that our association participated in a citizen's assembly. We hereby inform you that our association has not participated in any group or meeting recently. We are submitting this letter specifically to request that you make a correction to ensure accuracy.

The Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai Binding Industry Union, January 22nd.

Dear Editor,

We recently read in your newspaper's local news column on the 22nd of this month that our association received an urgent letter from the Hainan Qiongzhou Student Union branch, stating that French warships have arrived at Yulin Port in Yaxian County and are landing troops, forcibly recruiting locals as guides to search the sea, creating a precarious situation. The authorities in Qiong are turning a blind eye. They hoped to appeal to the National Government and publish the original letter in the newspaper to draw the attention of the Chinese people. We have not received any such news. Where did your newspaper obtain this information? Or is someone falsely using our association's name to spread rumors? We hope you will make a correction to clarify the situation.

Sincerely,

The Qiongya Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, January 22nd.

Dear Editor,

Today's newspaper carried an item titled "The Chunhua Rubber Factory Dispute Resolved," which we found very surprising. The fact is that in the case of the Chunhua factory engineer assaulting an apprentice, our association, out of humanitarian concerns, not only submitted a request to the Party and government authorities for investigation and handling but also hired a lawyer to prepare for legal action. Your newspaper stated that our association member He Penghui contacted Xu Haiquan, the factory's inspector, and proposed two conditions, stating that the factory had fully accepted them out of consideration for the apprentices. This is not true. Furthermore, Xu Haiquan and He Penghui only discussed the coal commission issue for the factory's long-term workers on the 21st, and they did not mention the abuse of apprentices. We are afraid that your newspaper's report is inaccurate. Therefore, we are writing this letter specifically to request that you make a correction to clarify the facts.

Sincerely,

The Shanghai First District Rubber Products Industry Union, January 21st.

Dear Editor,

Yesterday, we read a declaration from the Joint Federation of Trade Unions in your newspaper's news column, which included the name of the Soy Sauce Workers Union. Aside from our association, there are no other soy sauce worker organizations in this city with that name. However, our association did not send anyone to participate in the Joint Federation of Trade Unions beforehand, nor did we receive any notification. We fear that there may be misunderstandings in the outside world. Therefore, we are writing this letter specifically to request that you publish it in the "Letters" column.

Sincerely,

The Shanghai Soy Sauce Trade Union, January 21st.

Little Forum

The Fortunate Facilities of Shanghai Society 190

Walking down the street, opening your eyes to take a look, everywhere you see are things for eating, wearing, using, recreation, and entertainment. In terms of material enjoyment, everything is equipped for you meticulously and perfectly. There are dazzling department stores, extravagantly luxurious restaurants, tall Western-style hotels, bustling stages with gongs and drums, "refined entertainment" golf courses, openly gambling dog racing tracks and horse racing tracks, openly auctioned human flesh markets, dance halls, clubs, cinemas, teahouses, opium dens, gambling dens, and the "heaven and hell" worlds of ××. In short, in terms of eating, wearing, using, recreation, and entertainment, in Shanghai, you can say that you can have anything you want as long as you have a lot of money. Shanghai is pulling everyone down the road to ruin all day and night, constantly urging people to commit crimes and do evil. But when you have already fallen and become a so-called "scum" or "beggar," on the other hand, they have set up detention centers, prisons, or "foreign" jails for you. How meticulously equipped is Shanghai society!

However, here, you are only allowed to eat, wear, enjoy recreation, and entertainment, but you are not allowed to use your brain, you are not allowed to seek spiritual nourishment. If you don't believe me, in the vast Shanghai, you can only find one library attached to the Commercial Press, the Dongzhu Library. Can you find a second one?

I hear that London, Paris, New York, Tokyo, and every major city in the world has built large libraries, housing rich books for the people of the city to research and read. Perhaps this is the so-called "Western culture," and we Orientals should not learn the ways of foolish fools.

Every time I walk past × World and × Stage, I always have such a foolish thought in my heart: "When can this place be changed into a great and abundant library, and the people reading will still be so enthusiastic?"

Mass Literature

Pain · Silk 191

The five-year-old boy was clever and quick-witted, and was very much loved by his uncle. He played with his uncle all day long.

One day, he liked his uncle's small foreign knife, so he took it to play with. Carelessly, he cut his finger, dripped a few drops of blood, and cried for a long time from the pain.

This day, his uncle took him to a slaughterhouse to watch the pigs being slaughtered. He found it very novel and watched the various actions with wide eyes.

First, a strong butcher went to the back of the shed and pulled out a fat pig whose four hooves were tied up. He grabbed its tail with one hand and loosened it with the other. The pig was just shouting madly and struggling. He put it on a wide bench, and an assistant came over to help and hold it down. He casually took the sharp knife from the meat cutting table and tapped it twice on its throat with the back of the knife, making a gesture. Then, the tip of the knife turned and stabbed straight in. It shouted even more frantically and convulsed all over. When he pulled the knife out, the blood followed the tip of the knife and poured straight into the bucket on the ground.······

"Wah······" the boy suddenly cried loudly and dodged behind his uncle's knees. "It hurts!" he shouted.

His uncle quickly picked him up and asked him what hurt. While crying, he turned around and pointed to the wide bench with his finger. At this time, the fat pig was completely silent and motionless. His uncle understood and comforted him, saying, "Don't be afraid." The butcher also laughed and said, "This child is too timid. If he saw someone being killed, I don't know how scared he would be!"

The boy continued to cry, shouting "It hurts!" His uncle had no choice but to take him back. His parents were startled by his appearance and heard him shouting pain. Later, when they knew the reason, they were relieved. The father said, "What hurts! Your hand is not cut, the pain is on the pig!" His tone was scolding. The mother said, "Good boy, don't cry. Tomorrow we will buy its meat to eat for you. It is killed for people to eat." A piece of loving heart overflowed in words.

The child seemed not to have heard anything. He just kept crying and shouting pain.

Popular Science

The Structure of the Light Bulb Ding Xi 192

Fellow citizens! You live in this prosperous and lively city, and every night you see the electric lights on the streets, emitting brilliant light, much brighter than candles and kerosene lamps. Since you can see this good light, now you should know who invented this thing? What is its structure? If you don't know, please read this short article and you will understand.

In 1882, the American scientist Edison sealed a thin, white platinum wire in a glass bulb and applied electricity. When the current flowed, the platinum wire and the glass bulb were burned. At that time, he was very depressed because he could not think of a way to successfully manufacture the light bulb. However, he thought, "Nothing is difficult in the world, as long as you have the will." No matter what, he had to break through this difficulty and successfully manufacture the light bulb. He then experimented many times, using a pump to extract the air from the glass bulb, and then installing the platinum wire and applying electricity. It emitted brilliant light and could burn for a long time. At this time, the depression in his heart was relieved, and the light bulb was finally successfully manufactured.

Later, he thought that platinum wire was the most expensive metal in the world, several times more expensive than gold. Using it as a filament would not only limit sales in the future but also be too uneconomical. He began to re-improve it, using a kind of bamboo fiber, refining it into carbon filament, to replace the platinum wire. The results of the experiment showed that it was not only durable but also cheap. He then used this carbon filament to install in the light bulb.

Finally, he thought that although carbon filament was cheaper than platinum wire, the light emitted was not very bright and consumed a lot of electricity. So he again re-improved it and found that a kind of tungsten filament could be used to replace the carbon filament, which emitted strong light and was not expensive. Now this kind of tungsten filament bulb is popular in various countries.

The tungsten filament bulb is made of glass into a spherical shape, with a glass rod in the middle and a spiral continuous extremely fine tungsten filament. The two ends of the tungsten filament are connected to two thicker copper wires. One of these two copper wires is connected to the top of the bulb, and the other is connected to the side of the bulb. When lit, the current passes from one wire into the filament and out from the other wire. The resistance of tungsten filament is very large. When current passes through this conductor with large resistance, it turns into heat. When the heat reaches the extreme, it emits light.

Since tungsten filament has such a high temperature, why doesn't it burn out? This is because the air inside the bulb is extracted with a pump during manufacturing. There is no oxygen inside to support combustion, so the tungsten filament will not burn out due to heat. If we touch the outside of the light bulb with our hands, we only feel slightly warm. This is also because there is only sparse air inside the bulb, which transmits a small amount of heat, so our hands only feel slightly warm when we touch the bulb.

Street Sociology

Selling a Son Bai Hong 193

It was just the morning after a cold north wind had swept through, and the weather was extraordinarily cold. We took a tram all the way to the target range in the park to attend a meeting with a friend. On the way back, Mr. C hurriedly said to me, "I saw it for the first time! I saw it for the first time! Did you guys see it?"

I listened, not knowing what he was talking about, and quickly asked him what was the matter. He said, "Someone is actually selling his son at the end of North Sichuan Road!" Then, he said intermittently: I heard it at first and didn't pay attention, so I walked past. When I got to the foreign school, I could still hear his miserable cries very clearly in the twilight and the cold wind. He was shouting, 'Selling children! Does anyone want children?' That kind of sharp cry was too miserable, I couldn't bear to hear it! I couldn't bear to hear it!"

This is really too miserable, there is actually such a thing as selling children in the world. I asked him what the face of the person selling the child looked like. He said, "He is a tall man from the North with a rough and dark face. He was wearing a blue cloth gown and shouting high and low. There was a woman in her thirties next to him, holding a child in her arms, and three were squatting on the ground."

After saying that, everyone said in unison, "Woe is us!" Then someone said, "This person is a fool, just squatting at the quiet and unmanned end of North Sichuan Road to shout and sell. I am afraid that even if he freezes to death, no one will give him money. If he was on the main street, he could earn a sum of money!"

A few days later, the person selling his son suddenly came to shout and sell near our residence at dusk! The trembling, miserable cries wafted hesitantly in the darkness, startling me. Mr. C quickly said, "It's this person, his cries are the same as last time." So everyone pooled some money and gave it to him. They talked to each other, saying, "Really, this person can make a fortune in Shanghai by selling his son. Who would really go and buy his child?" "However, his selling his child is always real. If I go to buy, can he not sell it to me?" One of them said.

"Really," I thought in my heart too. The next evening, the person selling his son came again. He was still crying miserably on the street as he did yesterday, but no one paid attention to him. He was using his son to beg for money.

A friend said, "Chinese people are so poor that they sell their children, they still blame their own fate. They don't resent anyone for their suffering, which is painful enough!"

East, South, West, North

Shop Assistants Are Also Embarrassing 194

One day I broke into the ×× general merchandise store to buy something. The name I called was different from the name they called, so the thing that the shop assistant took out was not the thing I wanted to buy. I said to him, "It's not this one, please change it for me," but what did he say to me? "When you come to buy things next time, you must ask clearly first. You said it wrong and you want me to change it. It will cost me so much effort… Anyway, the same thing is delicious, isn't it almost the same?" I was very determined that he had to change it for me, and he finally changed it for me, but he was still grumbling endlessly.

Another time, I walked past a French bakery and casually bent in to buy a few breads. I saw a compatriot wearing a short jacket buying things there before me. On the counter in front of him, there were three big bags of bread. Later, when he calculated the bill, he said it was so expensive? I don't want it anymore. As a result, he bought a bread for two hundred cash. When he was about to leave, what did that Frenchman in the store do, you know? He still put on a smile and said a very strong Thank you.

At this time, I couldn't help but feel a strong feeling. Opening a store and being a boss, what do you use your shop assistants for standing in the counter for? Of course, it is to be the boss's hands and feet, to bring business to the boss. In that case, the patrons who come, no matter how much they trade, are customers of the store and must be warmly received and should not be offended for no reason. This is the business strategy.

It's nothing difficult to change something that was bought wrong, what's the big deal about costing so much effort, and talking a lot of nonsense; this is really infuriating. At the same time, seeing how politely foreigners do business, they filled three big bags of bread, and when they heard him say he didn't want them, they took them back without a word (and they didn't not know how to speak Chinese, nor did they not know how to speak angry words). Doesn't he cost effort?

Shop assistants! Want to attract patrons? You shouldn't treat customers with this attitude. Don't you need patrons? Ask your boss, what did you put up the signboard, open the door, and use your shop assistants for? I am not willing to be a foreign slave and willing to say that foreigners are good, but this is the way things really are.

Shanghai Stories

Shanghai Stories (17) Compiled and Translated by Zhou Rong 195

×The Battle of Mud City

Not long after the establishment of the Merchant Corps, conflict arose with the government troops. The Qing court specially appointed Ji'erhang'a, the Acting Provincial Surveillance Commissioner of Jiangsu, as the commander of the garrison at Xinzha. His command consisted of twenty to thirty thousand men. Ji'erhang'a was a Manchu and a civil official, originally ignorant of military affairs, but thought that commanding tens of thousands of troops would be an easy task. The Xinzha barracks were closely connected to the western end of the concession. A small number of soldiers sneaked into the concession, leading to minor conflicts with foreigners, which was expected. Soldiers also practiced shooting at targets to the west of the concession, with stray bullets occasionally hitting the area of today's racecourse and Xizang Road within the concession. Consequently, foreigners used this as an excuse to provoke the government troops. They initially demanded that General Ji'erhang'a move his camp to the south of the city, but Ji'erhang'a ignored them.

On the morning of April 4th, 1854 (the fourth year of Xianfeng), the British Consul Alcock sent a letter to Ji'erhang'a via Emerton, stating that the military camp at Xinzha must be moved by 4:00 PM. If the camp was not moved, they would attack with force. Ji'erhang'a replied, requesting that the matter of moving the camp be discussed at length and hoped that a dispute would not be hastily initiated. The foreigners then interpreted this reply as a rejection of their demand and, at 3:00 PM, summoned the Merchant Corps and foreign soldiers to gather in front of the British church, totaling 380 men. According to Captain Kelly of the American Plymouth, the circumstances of the foreign troops' assembly were recorded as follows:

"Our troops landed at 3:00 PM, totaling seventy-five men. The British troops who landed numbered two hundred. The Merchant Corps was entirely composed of British citizens, so they joined forces with the British troops. The American expatriates brought two field guns under my command, increasing our troops to one hundred men. The British troops then increased to two hundred and fifty men, and thirty sailors from American merchant ships joined our ranks."

At that time, the British and American troops and volunteers numbered no more than three hundred and eighty men, commanded by Captain O'Callaghan of the Encounter and his deputy Dew leading the British troops. Wade (T.F. Made, the British Vice-Consul), previously a Lieutenant-Deputy, commanded the Merchant Corps, and Kelly commanded the American troops.
